<rate>4<//rate><review>Strictly shotguns - - but every form of Shotgun-Sport is offered here.   Some decent instructors too.
I believe that you can rent shotguns from Triple-B.
Such outdoor/expansive facilities are bemcoing rare in So-Calif.   Enjoy this while you can.   Often beginners fire their first firearms in a confined (cinder-block) or concrete building with inadequate ventelation.  They end up next to another guy who rips off 50-rounds of 45-cal or 44mag.  This can traumatize beginners, especially how the concussions bounce off the nearby (hard surfaces.)
Don't underestimate how much more inviting a 20-gauge shotgun is outdoors with expansive fields and nobody messing with a second firearm next to them is.  This facility is almost a 35-year old anacrnism.  Other than electronic target counters, not much different than the 1984 Olympic facility for which much of this place was constructed.   But they do have a lunch grill and knowlegable  employees.  Plus a decent pro shop if you need a choke or vest.   BE PREPARED to take their SAFETY TEST if you're new to these sports.</review><pictures>None</pictures>< resp>

< Review>
I rated 4/5 and had a very good visit.

Pros - Nice environment with with a friendly staff. The office has a corky theme that dosent take itself too seriously. The staff and office were nice and very good with the kids. I never felt rushed, pressured or like "Just another patient".

Cons - The proccess was abit slow and some of the questions were abit personal. I felt like the staff was abit relaxed and the process was different than usual. I wasnt quite aware of some of the add-ons unitl I asked (Lenses) and my daughter loved kid frames but the size was wrong.

Summary - 5 stars would be VERY hard for me to give anyone. This place faced some obstacles with my visit but adapted at every turn. Even when my daughters frames didnt fit they dug into a shipment they just recieved. The lens person was very knowledgeable about any questions asked and even demonstrated differences. The eye doctor was equally knowledgeable and made the visit feel personally taylored to me. Thank you guys for finding a way to make my flex delay work and the outstanding visit.

Edit*
We were contacted Thursday or so. After paying a little over 1200.00 on monday I thought my glasses were in. I called nack Saturday only to be told that due to a misunderstanding my glasses were just being proccessed on Saturday. So even though the office got their money and messed up my 10 day wait started 6 days later.

No mention of anything to compensate or make things right. Appreantly once they have your money any burdens thereafter are all yours.

DISAPPOINTING.</Review>

We've been leaving our dachshund Sam at Thousand Hills Pet Resort for years.  I can tell you all about the staff and facility, but the best way for you to learn is to simply go check out the facility yourself.

The staff of Thousand Hills Pet Resort are wonderful.  You will have a hard time finding people more caring about animals and dedicated to their jobs.  My dog loves it here.  He is so happy to see the staff when we drop him off.  He plays off leash with the other ‚Äúmini‚Äù dogs all day long (they segregate the dogs by size and also by temperament).  Most of the staff recognize my dog by my car, even workers that I would swear I‚Äôve never met before.  They all greet him with excitement and treat him as if he was their own dog (and I‚Äôve observed this same behavior for all the dogs).

The play areas are great.  There is an open grassy area that they use for training (you can enroll your dog and they‚Äôll do some rudimentary training while he‚Äôs in daycare or boarding).  The fenced in areas where they spend most of their time (both boarding and daycare) are treated to eliminate fleas and ticks.  In the three years my dog has been going to Thousand Hills, he has never picked up fleas or a single tick.

The staff are very friendly with the humans, too.  I know most of them by name and they know me and my wife on sight.  They keep a computer record of all your telephone numbers and any medical history.  If your dog requires any medication and is staying overnight, it will be in their computer, on their checklists, and they‚Äôll take care of it.  If any issues arise, they'll call you.  They‚Äôll also notify you of any problems (such as your dog being anti-social in some way).

Best of all, there is ALWAYS someone from staff on site.  If you get nervous and want someone to check on your dog, all you have to do is call.< /Text>

<user_name>ahettena<//user_name><response>None</response>< Text>
I called Airmaxx when one of our furnaces ceased working.  The gentleman came the next morning, promptly diagnosed a malfunctioning gas valve, replaced it right away, and observed the system long enough to determine that a blockage in one of the ducts had caused the temperature to rise and the valve to fail.  He saw to that repair, and all was well.  The cost was quite reasonable, and he did not overcharge because of our address.

It turned out that someone working in the attic in the past stepped on and cracked the inside of the duct, and did not tell us.  This caused restricted the air flow and the cascade of events that led to failure of the gas valve.

Our system is 20 years old, and he explained the benefits and costs of maintaining vs. replacing furnaces.  All was done very professionally, without pressure, and I intend to engage Airmaxx to replace all 4 furnaces when the time is right.</Text>

<Pictures>None<//Pictures>< review>
Replaced our 30+ year old hvac with a new one from Airmaxx. We got  5 different quotes and they had the lowest price plus the best quality system (17.5 seer while all others were 14/16 seer). Sounded too good to be true, but the reviews online about them gave us confidence to choose them. I am glad we did as our new system is humming.

Pros:
1. Value - lowest price for a top notch system - furnace, A/C, and air purifier with a NEST thermostat too.
2. Carrier brand - our old system was Day and Night, which lasted over 30+ years so I wanted to go with the same brand/company.
3. Fast - Got the quote on Friday, and they installed the hvac on Monday.
4. Responsiveness - Edgar always responded very quickly to my emails. I prefer to talk over email so I have a paper trail.

Cons:
1. Both initial inspections failed. The duct inspection and city inspection both initially failed. Had to contact Airmaxx to have them come resolve the issue. Both issues were resolved at no cost so credit to Airmaxx for fixing it so quickly. Both inspections passed the 2nd time around, but obviously you wish the inspections would pass on first attempt.
2. Wish the workers wore shoe socks in the house.
3. I did notice my thermostat's fan function didn't work and it was because it needed an extra wire from the furnace to work. It did cost me a little extra to install because it required running  a wire through my cramped attic. I think the cost to install it was fair, but I wish it was discovered on the initial installation/estimate.

Overall, Airmaxx offered tremendous value compared to the other hvac installers so I'm very happy with my decision.<//review>

<review>Super yummy spot! Came here for lunch yesterday around 12:15 and only had to wait a few minutes after adding my group to the waitlist from Yelp while driving over. My boyfriend and I each got a lunch special and shared things. I‚Äôm vegetarian and there are lots of veggie options. The staff was flexible about changing the beef in the lunch special to tofu. Also got tofu pad thai and veggie rolls as the starter. My boyfriend had a beef starter. We both had Thai iced coffee and the only thing I will say is that it was REALLY sweet, I would probably recommend asking for it less sweet unless you just love things extremely sweet. <Review>Order to go food through Door Dash Tuesday, July 24. I ordered pad see ew with crispy pork belly and tom kha soup with chicken and mushrooms.

The delivery was reasonable and I have no complaints. The food was overpriced from typical Thai food prices. With tip and delivery fee, I paid $30 and some change for my food.

Of the two things I ordered, I liked the soup over the noodles. The soup had nice flavor and spice. In my opinion, I think the soup was light on the chicken and mushrooms. < Text>
A little disappointing that they did not have one of the more classic Thai desserts available, The Sweet Rice with Mango. However, this restaurant more than deserves 5 stars. Their curry was absolutely amazing! The coconut flavor in the curry was prevalent but not overpowering like most. This is the first place in years that I was able to finish all the curry without any meat left. Not as relevant to the foodies, nonetheless, the ginger tea that they serve is absolutely amazing. Flavorful and strong, yet it had a smooth finish. Overall, I would highly recommend this place to my closest friends and family.< /Text>

< Review>
A good spot with lot of tables inside. The lunch option is great and would recommend to go for the premium since it covers a drink as well. A bit disappointed with the spice level since the food for a bit bland compared to an authentic Thai place in terns of the spices. Service is affected during busy hours as we had to go down and request for service everytime we needed something at our table and we saw the same innearby tables as well. You might not face this problem if you are seated in the set of tables up front. Street parking is available plentiful in the vicinity and overall a good place for lunch. As recommended in yelp and opther online platforms, it is well advised to book your table before you reach since the place is of high demand on Fridays and weekends.</Review>

<user_id>115909617864159028876</user_id><username>Keong Hee</username>< Date>
1542270559443< /Date>
<rating>5<//rating>< review>
Ayara is my favorite Thai restaurant. This is actually my first Thai restaurant I ever recall going to. My coworkers & I ubered here & it was definitely worth the ride.

I loved it so much I introduced my other friends & boyfriend here. The only downfall is that it is a bit pricey. So be ready to spend some money. My boyfriend & I got three items from the menu. I ordered Papaya Salad, Crab Fried Rice & he ordered Spicy Chicken Basil. The order was an easy $50+.

The Papaya Salad is the best papaya salad I've had. I have visited many Thai restaurants trying all their crab & vegetable fried rice but no one, I repeat NO ONE tops Ayara! Their crab salad is made with REAL Dungeness Crab Meat. It's so freaking good. I top it off with the Thai Chilis in Fish Sauce. It's mouth watering good!

The service here is excellent! One time I ordered the Basil Fried Rice Mild Spicy & for some reason it was entirely too spicy for me (the chili peppers were probably extra spicy that season) & I asked if I could exchange it for the regular Basil Fried Rice & they exchanged it no questions asked or extra charge. I was so happy!!!!

I never had to wait more than 3 minutes for seating. The space looks small when you walk in, but then it opens up wider in the back. The decor is pretty cute too. My boyfriend loved it so much, he wanted to recreate the wall with the elephant/animal figurines.

If you are ever visiting in Los Angeles please go and visit Ayara. It is located near the Los Angeles airport. You will not regret it unless you forget your wallet lol! Now go make your palate happy! ^_^</review>

<text>As much as I really wanted to like this place I was very displeased with my order tonight. Although, the place was really cute inside and I bet has a lovely ambiance when open normally without COVID going on. But my togo order was very much lacking.

The soups flavor was ok but not flavorful. I had to add a ton of hot sauce to it to actually enjoy. All 3 maybe 4 wontons end up falling apart inside the soup. The container was very small, as you can see, for a $14 dollar soup. The veggies took up most of the container space. Even then still felt jipped.

The nice lady, who put in my order, was what I assumed pretty busy with an end of the night rush. She must of just forget to put in my utensils and napkins. I just assumed everything was there because the bag was folded up and taped. My suggestion next time maybe allow the customer to put in the contents of the soup at their discretion. This can help alleviate most of the problems. Sorry, I have to be that guy and write this review.< /text>< pictures>

< Text>
Look, I am a pilot for an American Airline. I have had Thai food all over the country, in fact all over the world. The food at this place is some of the best I've had in the United States. I found a place in Seattle that is better, but you can't go wrong with the food here. I always order the same thing. Green curry on the low spice side, prawns, and white rice. < review>
They need to figure out a better waitlist system.

We checked into the Yelp waitlist in advance. Arrived at the restaurant and checked in with the person at the front. At that point there was 7 people ahead of us on the list, and the expected wait was about 15 minutes. 50 minutes later, there's still 4 people on the list ahead of us, so we check back in with the front to see how much longer the wait will be. Turns out the person at the front has another list of names on a notepad, and says they've seen us waiting around for a while, so would put us at the top of the list. Appreciated the gesture, but it was too little, too late.

What's the point of having one waitlist on Yelp, and a totally different waitlist on paper? And how many times are you supposed to check in with the front to make sure you're on the _right_ waitlist? Maybe we'll stop back by for takeout sometime, but the dining in experience was a total bust.<//review>

<name>Jason Harrold</name><Time>1564075046356< /Time><Rating>4<//Rating><Text>Good FOOD!

Ive eaten here a few times, my wife has too even though we have never eaten here together we both agree that this is a nice Thai food gem.

You cant go wrong with the Pad Thai (shrimp), the Drunken noodles (if you like spicy) or Panaag or Red Curry.

I like spicy so those are my go toos.

Every time Ive been here for lunch the place has been PACKED i mean PACKED which in this case is because the food is great.

Service is friendly, this is a family owned business so I think theres more emphasis on the customer experience.

In the handful of times I have been here the food has always come out piping hot, just like I ordered, smooth service and great food.

Parking can be a bit of a pain in this area but there is a big lot close by.
Definitely check it out when you are in the neighborhood.
Great place to eat if you are in the mood for Thai<//Text>< pics>

< text>
Found this place taking my daughter to the airport.  Best pad thai noodles I have tried thus far. Not sure if it's a slight use of vinegar they use in it or what, but it's great. I squeeze some of the lime on top and it's bomb.  Next best thing I tried was their ayara fried rice with chicken. Incredible!  Had to other dishes, but I forgot what they were, because the pad Thai and ayara rice overshadowed them... Actually, it was the yellow curry (they called it something else that started with an "m". It has butternut squash and nuts. Tasty, but not the best we've had). Would definitely come back just for the rice and pad Thai.</text>

<rate>3</rate>< Review>
I was so excited to try Ayara based on the great reviews, however I must admit I was a bit disappointed.   I ordered the two dishes that were recommended.  Jade Curry and Pad Thai with a side of Peanut Sauce.   Let me start with the Jade Curry.  By itself, the jade curry was rather bland.   But when you mix it with the rice there is something that makes the curry come alive.  I'd give that a 4star rating.  It's the pad Thai that disappointed me the most.   It was dry amd the flavor was just average.   I did place my order to go, so possibly that contributed to my average food experience.  I will go back and give them a second chance, while trying some other dishes.   One thing to mention  is the parking.   It's always busy, even with a shopping parking lot nearby.< /Review>

< text>
Flavorful and delicious Thai food that either melts or explodes in your mouth. I recommend to try their Massaman beef curry, carmelized pork belly that melts in your mouth, and the Yaowaraj noodles that's satisfying.
The wait for a party of 4 on a Saturday night was about 30mins, and the staff kept us up to date about the availability of our table.
Service was prompt and responsive, at times giving us some piece of information about our meals. Towards the end of the meal, the owner approached us and asked about our dining experience.
Highly recommend this place if you happen to be in the area.<//text>

<response>None<//response>< Text>
This experience was wonderful.  It was close to the airport and easy to find. Our party of three on a Monday night ran into no wait, and we were surprised how comfortable (very not loud!) the atmosphere was.  The service was wonderful.  We never felt rushed, and never felt like we were waiting.

The three appetizers we got (When Tigers cry, Chicken Sate, and Royal Golden Baskets) were phenomenal, and our three entrees (Crazy Fish, Ka-Pow and the Soft shell crab special) were equally impressive.  I expected the prices to be higher for food of this quality.

This is one of those restaurants that's perfect to take friends from out of town, but given the low prices I'd also not hesitate going there any time I just wanted some amazing food.< /Text>

Even though several servers passed by inside, no one came out to check on us, so we went inside and waited on the empty bench. No one greeted us or even acknowledged our presence. We were waiting about 10 minutes when a group of people came in, and were immediately greeted warmly by an older Thai lady wearing a grey and white bandana  (the hostess?), and she asked them how many were in their party. I said, "Excuse me, but we have been waiting to be seated." I thought maybe they thought we were waiting on take out. She replied,  very nastily, "Yes, I know you are waiting. Don't get upset." I was very tIaken aback by her response,  since my tone was not rude at all.  She seated us shortly after that, but her attitude pretty much ruined the meal. My massaman curry was good, but not great. I counted maybe 5 peanuts and 3 potato chunks. My husband's wonton soup was good, but they brought it out several minutes before my meal came, so the soup got slightly cold waiting. Our waitress was polite and attentive, but it's too bad the hostess's rudeness ruined the meal. Needless to say,  we won't be going back.  I regret that this was my first experience with the LA food scene.  I hope it's not representative of what to expect from the rest of my stay.<//text>< Pics>

<Text>Ayara has been my favorite restaurant for years. Tonight my husband & I took his niece & her boyfriend there; they're visuting from Oregon. We all had a lovely meal. If I'd known Google was going to ask me for a review, I would have taken a picture of some of our food!</Text></record>

<pictures>None< /pictures><user_id>101132909266086505193<//user_id><time>1444508447813< /time><gmap_id>0x80c2b0cd606875b5:0x9b679271891c3125</gmap_id>< Text>
When it comes to food genres, Thai is not near the top of my list. That being said, I really like Ayara Thai. For me to really like a Thai place, when I'm not even a huge fan of the genre, the food must be pretty good.

Everything from the pad thai to the curries and soups is delicious at Ayara. If you make reservations ahead of time, they're good with handling medium-to-large sized groups. The service is always good and it's hard to go wrong with almost anything on the menu. You'll spend about $15-20 per person in the end, but everyone will be satisfied with the meal at one of LA's hidden Thai gems.<//Text>

<user_id>105895611862354145147<//user_id><Text>If you're on the Westside and don't want to drive over to Thai Town, this is a good Thai spot to go to. I always go for the lunch special. For $10, I got the combo #1 (chicken pad thai, chicken satay and a couple veggie rolls). This is great value and the taste definitely backs it up! Sprinkled some lime over the pad thai and it was delicious. The portion was very generous for a "lunch special" too.

If you're a fan of spicy, I'd suggest asking for the chili sauce to add a kick! We also got an order of the Tom Khah (coconut soup) and I was delighted by how rich the broth was. It wasn't too creamy either which was fantastic. A tad spicy but definitely tolerable.It made for a great pairing with the pad thai. Also, a lot of people complain about the parking. There is literally SO many spaces if you just park in the lot behind the store or in front of the Staples area. People can't expect to park directly in front of every store!! Get walking people!<//Text>< Pictures>
None</Pictures>
